	### Reconciliation ###

	shared_focus = {
		id = HLQ_reconciliation
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_liberty_statue
		x = -10
		y = 1
		offset = {
			x = 10
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = HLQ_reconciliation
			}
		}
		relative_position_id = HLQ_siegfrieds_retirement
		cost = 5.00
		prerequisite = { focus = HLQ_siegfrieds_retirement }
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = HLQ_status_quo }
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = HLQ_black_cloaks }

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 30
		}
		allow_branch = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
						option = HIDE
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = HLQ_status_quo
						has_completed_focus = HLQ_black_cloaks
					}
				}
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus HLQ_reconciliation"
			country_event = { id = hellquill.3 }
			hidden_effect = {
			    complete_national_focus = HLQ_wehrmacht
			}
			hidden_effect = { #collapse focus tree
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = hellquill_focus
					keep_completed = yes
				}
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
	}
